Model:     The repetitive invalid actions suggest a persistent issue with how `move_base` and `place` actions are constructed given the provided action instances. Let's re-examine the `basemotion` and `kin` predicates in the initial state very carefully, and try to find corresponding valid actions.
           
           The `basemotion` actions in the allowed list are structured as `(move_base Q_start Q_end TRAJ)`.
           The `kin` actions for `pick` and `place` are structured as `(kin A O P G Q T)`.
           
           Let's break down the process for each object:
           
           **Object v8 (currently at v9 on v11):**
           1. Robot needs to move to `q7` to pick `v8` at `v9`.
              - `atbconf(v3)` is true initially.
